</svg></section><section id="comprehensive---sensitive-specific-and-up-to-date" class="group/block relative sm:text-lg overflow-hidden py-20 white">  <div class="relative z-10 container"> <div class="max-w-content flex flex-col gap-8"> <h2 class="font-bold text-2xl sm:text-3xl"> Comprehensive - sensitive, specific, and up-to-date </h2> <div class="flex flex-col gap-16"> <ul class="grid-layout gap-y-16"> <li class="col-span-12 flex flex-col gap-6 md:col-span-4"> <svg width="46" height="46" class="h-8 w-8 sm:h-12 sm:w-12" data-icon="feather:eye">   <symbol id="ai:feather:eye" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><g fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"><path d="M1 12s4-8 11-8s11 8 11 8s-4 8-11 8s-11-8-11-8"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="3"/></g></symbol><use href="#ai:feather:eye"></use>  </svg> <h3 class="flex items-center gap-2 text-lg"> <span>Sensitive</span> </h3> <div class="space-y-6"> <p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>Detects all known hazards and predicted functional variants down to 30 b.p., preventing oligos too small to be screened by other methods from being used to assemble hazards</span></p>  </div> </li><li class="col-span-12 flex flex-col gap-6 md:col-span-4"> <svg width="46" height="46" class="h-8 w-8 sm:h-12 sm:w-12" data-icon="feather:target">   <symbol id="ai:feather:target" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><g fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="6"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="2"/></g></symbol><use href="#ai:feather:target"></use>  </svg> <h3 class="flex items-center gap-2 text-lg"> <span>Specific</span> </h3> <div class="space-y-6"> <p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>Outputs ~0 false alarms by using patented reverse screening to remove known non-hazards, enabling use in synthesizers and assemblers without human support</span></p>  </div> </li><li class="col-span-12 flex flex-col gap-6 md:col-span-4"> <svg width="46" height="46" class="h-8 w-8 sm:h-12 sm:w-12" data-icon="feather:refresh-cw">   <symbol id="ai:feather:refresh-cw" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><g fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"><path d="M23 4v6h-6M1 20v-6h6"/><path d="M3.51 9a9 9 0 0 1 14.85-3.36L23 10M1 14l4.64 4.36A9 9 0 0 0 20.49 15"/></g></symbol><use href="#ai:feather:refresh-cw"></use>  </svg> <h3 class="flex items-center gap-2 text-lg"> <span>Up-to-date</span> </h3> <div class="space-y-6"> <p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>Uses a centralized database, updated swiftly by our biosecurity team as new threats are identified; no need to update local installations</span></p>  </div> </li> </ul> </div> </div> </div>  </section><section id="trustworthy---privacy-preserving-and-neutral" class="group/block relative sm:text-lg overflow-hidden py-20 white">  <div class="relative z-10 container"> <div class="max-w-content flex flex-col gap-8"> <h2 class="font-bold text-2xl sm:text-3xl"> Trustworthy - privacy-preserving and neutral </h2> <div class="flex flex-col gap-16"> <ul class="grid-layout gap-y-16"> <li class="col-span-12 flex flex-col gap-6 md:col-span-4"> <svg width="46" height="46" class="h-8 w-8 sm:h-12 sm:w-12" data-icon="feather:lock">   <symbol id="ai:feather:lock" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><g fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"><rect width="18" height="11" x="3" y="11" rx="2" ry="2"/><path d="M7 11V7a5 5 0 0 1 10 0v4"/></g></symbol><use href="#ai:feather:lock"></use>  </svg> <h3 class="flex items-center gap-2 text-lg"> <span>Privacy-preserving</span> </h3> <div class="space-y-6"> <p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>Protected by multiple layers of cryptography &amp; distributed around the world, your customers’ sequences will be uninterpretable - by us or anyone else</span></p>  </div> </li><li class="col-span-12 flex flex-col gap-6 md:col-span-4"> <svg width="46" height="46" class="h-8 w-8 sm:h-12 sm:w-12" data-icon="feather:globe">   <symbol id="ai:feather:globe" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><g fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><path d="M2 12h20M12 2a15.3 15.3 0 0 1 4 10a15.3 15.3 0 0 1-4 10a15.3 15.3 0 0 1-4-10a15.3 15.3 0 0 1 4-10"/></g></symbol><use href="#ai:feather:globe"></use>  </svg> <h3 class="flex items-center gap-2 text-lg"> <span>Politically neutral</span> </h3> <div class="space-y-6"> <p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>Run within a Swiss non-profit foundation without involvement by any government - a worldwide research collaboration</span></p>  </div> </li> </ul> </div> </div> </div>  </section><section class="group/block relative sm:text-lg overflow-hidden py-20 white">  <div class="relative z-10 container"> <div class="max-w-content flex flex-col gap-8">  <div class="flex flex-col gap-16"> <div class="space-y-6"> <figure class="py-4"><img class="object-cover" width="955" height="481" loading="lazy" decoding="async" src="/_astro/dna-synthesis-order_Z1klCLk.webp" srcset="/_astro/dna-synthesis-order_DuWAa.webp 272w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_Z1fnWNc.webp 512w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_Z1talle.webp 614w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_137yCx.webp 816w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_2hTWFR.webp 1024w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_bzqm3.webp 1229w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_Z1x2TlG.webp 1536w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_xu6Di.webp 1638w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_Z1wqXE4.webp 1843w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_Z1KHgC5.webp 2048w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_ZQLJqk.webp 2458w, /_astro/dna-synthesis-order_ZQvYJ4.webp 3072w" sizes="80vw" alt="Diagram showing orders being split into subsequences, one-way-encrypted, and compared to an encrypted hazards database"></figure><p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span></span></p>  </div> </div> </div> </div>  </section><section id="detailed-description-of-the-platform" class="group/block relative sm:text-lg overflow-hidden py-20 light">  <div class="relative z-10 container"> <div class="max-w-content flex flex-col gap-8"> <h2 class="font-bold text-2xl sm:text-3xl"> Detailed description of the platform </h2> <div class="flex flex-col gap-16"> <div class="space-y-6"> <p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>The SecureDNA system uses a novel exact-match search algorithm that finds matches to hazards and functional equivalents. It does this by generating the set of all hazard subsequences of a predefined length, choosing some to defend quasi-randomly, then using algorithms to generate millions of functionally equivalent subsequences of each. These are subjected to reverse screening by comparing them to existing sequence databases in order to remove any that match known non-hazardous entries.</span></p><p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>The reverse screening step virtually eliminates false positives, the inclusion of quasi-random functional variants prevents adversaries from redesigning or mutating the hazard to evade screening, and searching for  30 base pair subsequences makes it very difficult to assemble hazards from oligonucleotides that are too small to be screened using other methods.</span></p><p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>Because exact-match screening is computationally efficient, we can apply oblivious multi-party cryptography to protect the confidentiality of both orders and the hazard database. Using this scheme, each possible subsequence of an order to be screened is turned into a unique cryptographic hash, and each such hash is then looked up in the database of hazards.</span></p><p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>This hash requires multiple separate machines to compute, meaning that even an attacker who could eavesdrop on network traffic or compromise a subset of computers in the screening system could not learn the plaintext of a customer order, and not even SecureDNA itself ever receives the customer’s DNA sequences—they remain safely on-premises at a provider or within the hardware of a benchtop synthesizer.</span></p><p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>Screening for hazardous DNA sequences is provided as a free service by the SecureDNA Foundation, an independent nonprofit foundation in the sense of Article 80 et seqq. Swiss Civil Code with legal seat in Zug, Switzerland. The purpose of the Foundation is to develop, maintain, administrate, distribute, and encourage the universal adoption of software for screening nucleic acid sequences. The Foundation may support any action intended to prevent nucleic acids from being used to cause harm.</span></p>  </div> </div> </div> </div>  </section><section id="partners-and-support" class="group/block relative sm:text-lg overflow-hidden py-20 white">  <div class="relative z-10 container"> <div class="max-w-content flex flex-col gap-8"> <h2 class="font-bold text-2xl sm:text-3xl"> Partners and Support </h2> <div class="flex flex-col gap-16"> <div class="space-y-6"> <p class="group/paragraph max-w-prose"><span>We are grateful for support from the Open Philanthropy Project to team members at MIT, Aarhus University, and Northeastern University, and to an anonymous Chinese philanthropist for a donation to team members at Tsinghua University and Shanghai Jiao Tong University.</span></p>  </div><ul class="grid-layout"> <li class="col-span-4 flex flex-col items-center justify-center md:col-span-2"> <img class="aspect-video object-contain object-center"
